VerifyAdmissionResponse(uid types.UID, mutating bool, review runtime.Object) (*AdmissionResponse, error) {\n\tswitch r := review.(type) {\n\tcase *admissionv1.AdmissionReview:\n\t\tif r.Response ==     patch,\n\t\t\tPatchType:        patchType,\n\t\t\tResult:           r.Response.Result,\n\t\t\tWarnings:         r.Response.Warnings,\n\t\t}, nil\n\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, responses. The implementation is located in the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver package.\\n\\n## Webhook Admission Controllers\\n\\nThe two admission webhook plugins are defined in:\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Implements the Plugin type which satisfies admission.MutationInterface. The NewMutatingWebhook function creates an instance, and the Plugin.Admit method is the entry point called during API server admission.\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Implements the Plugin type which satisfies admission.ValidationInterface. The NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook function creates an instance, and the Plugin.Validate method is the entry point.\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Base\\n\\nBoth plugins inherit from the generic Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go), which provides the core dispatch infrastructure. The Webhook.Dispatch method is the central dispatcher that orchestrates the entire webhook invocation chain. The Webhook.ShouldCallHook method determines whether a specific webhook should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, rule matching, and match conditions.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nThe actual dispatch of webhook calls to remote servers is handled by type-specific dispatchers:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): The Dispatch method iterates through configured mutating webhooks in sequence. For each applicable webhook, it calls callAttrMutatingHook which constructs the admission request, invokes the webhook, verifies the response, and applies any JSON patches returned.\\n- **validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): The Dispatch method collects all relevant webhooks upfront and invokes them in parallel using goroutines. The callHook method constructs the request, calls the webhook, and verifies the response. Validation errors are aggregated and returned.\\n\\n## Request and Response Handling\\n\\nThe staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go module manages admission review object creation and response verification:\\n- **CreateAdmissionObjects** function creates the AdmissionReview request objects (supporting both v1 and v1beta1 versions) to send to webhooks.\\n- **CreateV1AdmissionReview** and **CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview** construct versioned admission review requests from the admission attributes.\\n- **VerifyAdmissionResponse** validates webhook responses and extracts the AdmissionResponse containing audit annotations, the allow/deny decision, patches (for mutating webhooks), and warnings.\\n\\n## Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nFor mutating webhooks, the mutatingDispatcher applies patches sequentially and tracks which webhooks mutated the object. It handles reinvocation of webhooks when earlier mutations trigger reinvocation policies.\\n\\nFor validating webhooks, the validatingDispatcher aggregates validation results from parallel webhook invocations and returns the first encountered error.\\n\\n## Configuration Management\\n\\nWebhook configurations are dynamically managed by:\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go): Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active mutating webhooks.\\n- **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go): Watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active validating webhooks.\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\nAdditional components supporting the webhook chain include:\\n- **Webhook Accessors** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go): Provides the WebhookAccessor interface for accessing webhook configuration properties.\\n- **Predicate Matchers**: Namespace matcher, object matcher, and rule matcher evaluate whether a webhook should be invoked for a given request.\\n- **Match Conditions** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go): Evaluates CEL-based match conditions.\\n- **Error Handling** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/statuserror.go): Converts webhook failures into appropriate API errors.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":322,"cache_read_input_tokens":61883,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":322},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"17af4e3e-8bc9-4e6e-b4f0-fcad2a086335","uuid":"9e9c4867-98f6-466c-bb99-2b000fb05898"}

\"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of two main admission controllers (mutating and validating) and a sophisticated dispatch mechanism that aggregates webhook responses. The implementation is located in the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver package.\\n\\n## Webhook Admission Controllers\\n\\nThe two admission webhook plugins are defined in:\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Implements the Plugin type which satisfies admission.MutationInterface. The NewMutatingWebhook function creates an instance, and the Plugin.Admit method is the entry point called during API server admission.\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Implements the Plugin type which satisfies admission.ValidationInterface. The NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook function creates an instance, and the Plugin.Validate method is the entry point.\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Base\\n\\nBoth plugins inherit from the generic Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go), which provides the core dispatch infrastructure. The Webhook.Dispatch method is the central dispatcher that orchestrates the entire webhook invocation chain. The Webhook.ShouldCallHook method determines whether a specific webhook should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, rule matching, and match conditions.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nThe actual dispatch of webhook calls to remote servers is handled by type-specific dispatchers:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): The Dispatch method iterates through configured mutating webhooks in sequence. For each applicable webhook, it calls callAttrMutatingHook which constructs the admission request, invokes the webhook, verifies the response, and applies any JSON patches returned.\\n- **validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): The Dispatch method collects all relevant webhooks upfront and invokes them in parallel using goroutines. The callHook method constructs the request, calls the webhook, and verifies the response. Validation errors are aggregated and returned.\\n\\n## Request and Response Handling\\n\\nThe staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go module manages admission review object creation and response verification:\\n- **CreateAdmissionObjects** function creates the AdmissionReview request objects (supporting both v1 and v1beta1 versions) to send to webhooks.\\n- **CreateV1AdmissionReview** and **CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview** construct versioned admission review requests from the admission attributes.\\n- **VerifyAdmissionResponse** validates webhook responses and extracts the AdmissionResponse containing audit annotations, the allow/deny decision, patches (for mutating webhooks), and warnings.\\n\\n## Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nFor mutating webhooks, the mutatingDispatcher applies patches sequentially and tracks which webhooks mutated the object. It handles reinvocation of webhooks when earlier mutations trigger reinvocation policies.\\n\\nFor validating webhooks, the validatingDispatcher aggregates validation results from parallel webhook invocations and returns the first encountered error.\\n\\n## Configuration Management\\n\\nWebhook configurations are dynamically managed by:\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go): Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active mutating webhooks.\\n- **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go): Watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active validating webhooks.\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\nAdditional components supporting the webhook chain include:\\n- **Webhook Accessors** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go): Provides the WebhookAccessor interface for accessing webhook configuration properties.\\n- **Predicate Matchers**: Namespace matcher, object matcher, and rule matcher evaluate whether a webhook should be invoked for a given request.\\n- **Match Conditions** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go): Evaluates CEL-based match conditions.\\n- **Error Handling** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/statuserror.go): Converts webhook failures into appropriate API errors.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

\"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of two main admission controllers (mutating and validating) and a sophisticated dispatch mechanism that aggregates webhook responses. The implementation is located in the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver package.\\n\\n## Webhook Admission Controllers\\n\\nThe two admission webhook plugins are defined in:\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Implements the Plugin type which satisfies admission.MutationInterface. The NewMutatingWebhook function creates an instance, and the Plugin.Admit method is the entry point called during API server admission.\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Implements the Plugin type which satisfies admission.ValidationInterface. The NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook function creates an instance, and the Plugin.Validate method is the entry point.\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Base\\n\\nBoth plugins inherit from the generic Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go), which provides the core dispatch infrastructure. The Webhook.Dispatch method is the central dispatcher that orchestrates the entire webhook invocation chain. The Webhook.ShouldCallHook method determines whether a specific webhook should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, rule matching, and match conditions.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nThe actual dispatch of webhook calls to remote servers is handled by type-specific dispatchers:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): The Dispatch method iterates through configured mutating webhooks in sequence. For each applicable webhook, it calls callAttrMutatingHook which constructs the admission request, invokes the webhook, verifies the response, and applies any JSON patches returned.\\n- **validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): The Dispatch method collects all relevant webhooks upfront and invokes them in parallel using goroutines. The callHook method constructs the request, calls the webhook, and verifies the response. Validation errors are aggregated and returned.\\n\\n## Request and Response Handling\\n\\nThe staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go module manages admission review object creation and response verification:\\n- **CreateAdmissionObjects** function creates the AdmissionReview request objects (supporting both v1 and v1beta1 versions) to send to webhooks.\\n- **CreateV1AdmissionReview** and **CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview** construct versioned admission review requests from the admission attributes.\\n- **VerifyAdmissionResponse** validates webhook responses and extracts the AdmissionResponse containing audit annotations, the allow/deny decision, patches (for mutating webhooks), and warnings.\\n\\n## Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nFor mutating webhooks, the mutatingDispatcher applies patches sequentially and tracks which webhooks mutated the object. It handles reinvocation of webhooks when earlier mutations trigger reinvocation policies.\\n\\nFor validating webhooks, the validatingDispatcher aggregates validation results from parallel webhook invocations and returns the first encountered error.\\n\\n## Configuration Management\\n\\nWebhook configurations are dynamically managed by:\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go): Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active mutating webhooks.\\n- **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go): Watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active validating webhooks.\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\nAdditional components supporting the webhook chain include:\\n- **Webhook Accessors** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go): Provides the WebhookAccessor interface for accessing webhook configuration properties.\\n- **Predicate Matchers**: Namespace matcher, object matcher, and rule matcher evaluate whether a webhook should be invoked for a given request.\\n- **Match Conditions** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go): Evaluates CEL-based match conditions.\\n- **Error Handling** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/statuserror.go): Converts webhook failures into appropriate API errors.\"\n}\n","numLines":174,"startLine":1,"totalLines":174}}}
